	scout_car_chassis = {
		year = 1936

		is_archetype = yes
		is_buildable = no
		is_convertable = yes
		picture = archetype_light_tank_equipment
		type = armor
		group_by = archetype

		max_military_factories = 75

		interface_category = interface_category_armor
		priority = 1000

		can_be_produced = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = BUL_treaty_of_neuilly_sur_seine
				has_idea = HUN_treaty_of_trianon
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = AI_purge_scout_car_chassis_production
			}
		}
		#Misc Abilities
		maximum_speed = 1
		reliability = 0
		max_strength = 1

		#Defensive Abilities
		defense = 1
		breakthrough = 1
		hardness = 0
		armor_value = 1

		#Offensive Abilities
		soft_attack = 1
		hard_attack = 1
		ap_attack = 1
		air_attack = 0

		#Space taken in convoy
		lend_lease_cost = 0.6

		build_cost_ic = 8
		fuel_consumption = 1.0
		resources = {
			steel = 2
			rubber = 1
			coal = 4
		}

		module_slots = {
			main_armament_slot = {
				required = yes
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_tiny_main_armament
				}
			}
			turret_type_slot = {
				required = yes
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_tiny_turret_type
				}
			}
			engine_type_slot = {
				required = yes
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_tiny_engine_type
				}
			}
			suspension_type_slot = {
				required = yes
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_light_suspension_type
					tank_heavy_suspension_type
				}
			}

			special_type_slot_1 = {
				required = no
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_special_module
					tank_radio_module
				}
			}

			special_type_slot_2 = {
				required = no
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_special_module
				}
			}
		}
		default_modules = {
			main_armament_slot = empty
			turret_type_slot = empty
			engine_type_slot = empty
			suspension_type_slot = empty
			#special_type_slot_1 = armour_piercing
			special_type_slot_1 = empty
			special_type_slot_2 = empty
		}
		module_count_limit = { category = tank_radio_module count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { category = tank_secondary_turret count < 2 }
		#module_count_limit = { module = amphibious_drive count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = tank_crew_radios count < 2 }
